Here's a comprehensive breakdown of the key components:\\n\\n## 1. Abstract CertValidator Interface\\n**File**: `source/common/tls/cert_validator/cert_validator.h`\\n\\nDefines the `CertValidator` abstract class with pure virtual methods:\\n- `addClientValidationContext()`: Configures client certificate validation for an SSL context\\n- `doVerifyCertChain()`: Performs the main certificate chain verification (can be asynchronous)\\n- `initializeSslContexts()`: Initializes SSL contexts with validation configuration\\n- `updateDigestForSessionId()`: Updates hash for session ID calculation based on validation config\\n- Helper methods for retrieving CA certificate info and expiration times\\n\\nThe `ValidationResults` struct carries status (Pending, Successful, Failed), detailed status, TLS alerts, and error details.\\n\\n## 2. DefaultCertValidator (X.509 Chain Verification)\\n**Files**: `source/common/tls/cert_validator/default_validator.h`, `.cc`\\n\\nThe `DefaultCertValidator` class implements the CertValidator interface for standard X.509 certificate validation:\\n- **Chain Verification**: Uses OpenSSL/BoringSSL X509_STORE_CTX for X.509 chain validation\\n- **Certificate Pinning**: `verifyCertificateHashList()` for SHA-256 hash-based pinning\\n- **SPKI Pinning**: `verifyCertificateSpkiList()` for Subject Public Key Information pinning\\n- **SAN Verification**: `verifySubjectAltName()` for string-based SAN matching and `matchSubjectAltName()` for pattern-based matching\\n- **CRL Support**: Handles certificate revocation lists loaded from CA certificates\\n- **Configuration**: Supports trust verification, untrusted certificate acceptance, and certificate hash lists\\n\\nThe factory class `DefaultCertValidatorFactory` creates instances of DefaultCertValidator.\\n\\n## 3. SAN Matcher (Subject Alternative Name Matching)\\n**Files**: `source/common/tls/cert_validator/san_matcher.h`, `.cc`\\n\\nImplements flexible Subject Alternative Name matching:\\n- **SanMatcher Interface**: Pure virtual `match()` method for checking if a GENERAL_NAME matches criteria\\n- **StringSanMatcher Class**: Concrete implementation supporting multiple SAN types:\\n  - `GEN_DNS`: Domain name matching with wildcard support and regex patterns\\n  - `GEN_URI`: URI matching\\n  - `GEN_EMAIL`: Email address matching\\n  - `GEN_IPADD`: IP address matching\\n  - `GEN_OTHERNAME`: OID-based \\\"Other Name\\\" matching with custom ASN.1 objects\\n- **createStringSanMatcher()**: Factory function that creates appropriate matchers based on `SubjectAltNameMatcher` protobuf configuration\\n- Uses `StringMatcherImpl` for flexible pattern matching (exact, prefix, suffix, regex, contains)\\n\\n## 4. ContextImpl (TLS Context Management)\\n**Files**: \\n- `source/common/tls/context_impl.h`, `.cc`: Base implementation\\n- `source/common/tls/client_context_impl.h`, `.cc`: Client-side specialization\\n- `source/common/tls/server_context_impl.h`, `.cc`: Server-side specialization\\n\\nThe `ContextImpl` class manages:\\n- **TLS Contexts**: Maintains `std::vector<Ssl::TlsContext> tls_contexts_` where each contains:\\n  - `ssl_ctx_`: BoringSSL SSL_CTX\\n  - `cert_chain_`: X509 certificate chain\\n  - `ocsp_response_`: Unique OCSP response wrapper\\n  - `is_ecdsa_`, `is_must_staple_`: Certificate properties\\n- **Certificate Validator**: Holds `CertValidatorPtr cert_validator_` for performing validations\\n- **Custom Verify Callback**: Static `customVerifyCallback()` for asynchronous certificate validation\\n- **OCSP Support**: `secondsUntilFirstOcspResponseExpires()` queries OCSP response expiration\\n- **Asynchronous Validation**: `customVerifyCertChain()` and `customVerifyCertChainForQuic()` for async cert validation\\n\\nServerContextImpl additionally handles:\\n- OCSP stapling with policies (Lenient, Strict, Must Staple)\\n- `ocspStapleAction()`: Determines whether to staple OCSP response based on client capabilities\\n- Server Name Indication (SNI) based certificate selection\\n- TLS context selection via `selectTlsContext()` and `findTlsContext()` methods\\n\\n## 5. OCSP Response Parsing and Stapling\\n**Files**: `source/common/tls/ocsp/ocsp.h`, `.cc`, `asn1_utility.h`, `.cc`\\n\\nComprehensive OCSP (Online Certificate Status Protocol) support:\\n- **OcspResponse Structure**: Top-level DER-encoded OCSP response containing status and response data\\n- **OcspResponseStatus Enum**: Reflects RFC 6960 status codes (Successful, MalformedRequest, InternalError, TryLater, SigRequired, Unauthorized)\\n- **BasicOcspResponse**: Implements the standard OCSP response format with single certificate status per response\\n- **OcspResponseWrapperImpl**: Wraps DER-encoded OCSP responses and provides:\\n  - `matchesCertificate()`: Verifies response is for a specific certificate\\n  - `isExpired()`: Checks if response's nextUpdate has passed\\n  - `secondsUntilExpiration()`: Calculates time until expiration\\n  - `getThisUpdate()`, `getNextUpdate()`: Validity window accessors\\n- **Asn1OcspUtility**: ASN.1 parsing utilities for OCSP structures:\\n  - `parseOcspResponse()`: Parses DER-encoded OCSP response\\n  - `parseResponseStatus()`: Extracts OCSP response status\\n  - `parseResponseBytes()`: Parses response data\\n  - `parseBasicOcspResponse()`: Parses BasicOcspResponse structure\\n\\nOCSP responses are stored in `TlsContext::ocsp_response_` and ServerContextImpl manages stapling policies in `server_context_impl.h` using `OcspStaplePolicy` (Lenient, Strict, MustStaple).\\n\\n## 6. SPIFFE Validator (Alternative Implementation)\\n**Files**: `source/extensions/transport_sockets/tls/cert_validator/spiffe/spiffe_validator.h`, `.cc`\\n\\nAlternative CertValidator implementation for verification\\n- `extractTrustDomain()`: Parses SPIFFE identity from URI SANs\\n- `certificatePrecheck()`: Validates certificate structure before chain verification\\n- `matchSubjectAltName()`: Uses SAN matchers for SPIFFE-specific validation\\n- Supports expired certificate allowance for testing\\n\\n## Integration Flow\\n\\nThe complete pipeline works as follows:\\n1. **Initialization**: ContextImpl creates a CertValidator (typically DefaultCertValidator) and calls `initializeSslContexts()`\\n2. **Handshake**: During TLS handshake, OpenSSL invokes the custom verify callback registered with `SSL_CTX_set_custom_verify()`\\n3. **Validation**: ContextImpl's `customVerifyCallback()` delegates to `doVerifyCertChain()` on the CertValidator\\n4. **Chain Verification**: DefaultCertValidator performs X.509 chain validation using X509_STORE_CTX\\n5. **SAN Matching**: After chain verification, StringSanMatchers validate the certificate's Subject Alternative Names\\n6. **Async Handling**: For async validators, ValidateResultCallback is invoked when validation completes\\n7. **OCSP Support**: ServerContextImpl manages OCSP responses, checking expiration via OcspResponseWrapperImpl\\n8. **Result**: ValidationResults with status and error details are returned to the SSL library\\n\\nThis architecture provides a flexible, pluggable certificate validation system supporting standard X.509 validation, SPIFFE identity verification, OCSP stapling, and custom validation OCSP Response Parsing and Stapling\\n**Files**: `source/common/tls/ocsp/ocsp.h`, `.cc`, `asn1_utility.h`, `.cc`\\n\\nComprehensive OCSP (Online Certificate Status Protocol) support:\\n- **OcspResponse Structure**: Top-level DER-encoded OCSP response containing status and response data\\n- **OcspResponseStatus Enum**: Reflects RFC 6960 status codes (Successful, MalformedRequest, InternalError, TryLater, SigRequired, Unauthorized)\\n- **BasicOcspResponse**: Implements the standard OCSP response format with single certificate status per response\\n- **OcspResponseWrapperImpl**: Wraps DER-encoded OCSP responses and provides:\\n  - `matchesCertificate()`: Verifies response is for a specific certificate\\n  - `isExpired()`: Checks if response's nextUpdate has passed\\n  - `secondsUntilExpiration()`: Calculates time until expiration\\n  - `getThisUpdate()`, `getNextUpdate()`: Validity window accessors\\n- **Asn1OcspUtility**: ASN.1 parsing utilities for OCSP structures:\\n  - `parseOcspResponse()`: Parses DER-encoded OCSP response\\n  - `parseResponseStatus()`: Extracts OCSP response status\\n  - `parseResponseBytes()`: Parses response data\\n  - `parseBasicOcspResponse()`: Parses BasicOcspResponse structure\\n\\nOCSP responses are stored in `TlsContext::ocsp_response_` and ServerContextImpl manages stapling policies in `server_context_impl.h` using `OcspStaplePolicy` (Lenient, Strict, MustStaple).\\n\\n## 6. SPIFFE Validator (Alternative Implementation)\\n**Files**: `source/extensions/transport_sockets/tls/cert_validator/spiffe/spiffe_validator.h`, `.cc`\\n\\nAlternative CertValidator implementation for SPIFFE (Secure Production Identity Framework For Everyone):\\n- Extends CertValidator interface for trust bundle-based validation\\n- `trustBundleStores()`: Maintains per-trust-domain X509_STORE for verification\\n- `extractTrustDomain()`: Parses SPIFFE identity from URI SANs\\n- `certificatePrecheck()`: Validates certificate structure before chain verification\\n- `matchSubjectAltName()`: Uses SAN matchers for SPIFFE-specific validation\\n- Supports expired certificate allowance for testing\\n\\n## Integration Flow\\n\\nThe complete pipeline works as follows:\\n1. **Initialization**: ContextImpl creates a CertValidator (typically DefaultCertValidator) and calls `initializeSslContexts()`\\n2. **Handshake**: During TLS handshake, OpenSSL invokes the custom verify callback registered with `SSL_CTX_set_custom_verify()`\\n3. **Validation**: ContextImpl's `customVerifyCallback()` delegates to `doVerifyCertChain()` on the CertValidator\\n4. **Chain Verification**: DefaultCertValidator performs X.509 chain validation using X509_STORE_CTX\\n5. **SAN Matching**: After chain verification, StringSanMatchers validate the certificate's Subject Alternative Names\\n6. **Async Handling**: For async validators, ValidateResultCallback is invoked when validation completes\\n7. **OCSP Support**: ServerContextImpl manages OCSP responses, checking expiration via OcspResponseWrapperImpl\\n8. **Result**: ValidationResults with status and error details are returned to the SSL library\\n\\nThis architecture provides a flexible, pluggable certificate validation system supporting standard X.509 validation, SPIFFE identity verification, OCSP stapling, and custom validation logic.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
